Base directory for this skill: /Users/duongntd99/Documents/Personal/strawberry-agents/.claude/skills/pre-compact-save

# /pre-compact-save ‚Äî Pre-Compact Memory Consolidation

## When to use

- Before running `/compact` on an Evelynn or Sona coordinator session
- When the PreCompact hook blocks `/compact` and asks you to consolidate first
- When you want a mid-session snapshot without ending the session

## When NOT to use

- Subagent sessions (out of scope ‚Äî Lissandra only handles coordinator sessions)
- Actual session end (use `/end-session` instead ‚Äî it produces the full transcript archive)
- Immediately after a recent consolidation (redundant; worst case it produces a duplicate)

## Arguments

`` (optional): `evelynn` or `sona` to override auto-detection. Empty ‚Üí auto-detect from session greeting.

## Protocol

1. **Preflight.**
   - Read the session jsonl path: `~/.claude/projects/<project-slug>/<session-id>.jsonl`. Derive `session_id` and `transcript_path` from the current environment.
   - If `` is non-empty, use it as the coordinator. Otherwise detect:
     - Scan the first 3 user messages for `Hey Sona` (case-insensitive) ‚Üí coordinator = `sona`
     - Otherwise coordinator = `evelynn` (repo default per CLAUDE.md Caller Routing)
   - Cross-check `[concern: work]` vs `[concern: personal]` tags on subagent prompts. Contradiction ‚Üí refuse with a diagnostic.

2. **Spawn Lissandra** via the Agent tool with `subagent_type: "Lissandra"`. Note: Lissandra updates `open-threads.md` and regenerates `INDEX.md` as part of the coordinator shard write, same as `/end-session` Step 6b. Prompt shape:

   ```
   [concern: <personal|work>]

   Consolidate this coordinator session before /compact. You are impersonating <coordinator>.

   - session_id: <uuid>
   - transcript_path: <absolute path to jsonl>
   - coordinator: <evelynn|sona>

   Run the full protocol in your agent definition (handoff shard, session shard, conditional learnings, journal entry, optional transcript excerpt, commit, sentinel). Write to `agents/<coordinator>/...` directories only. Use the coordinator's first-person voice.

   Report back with: artifact paths, commit SHA, push status, skipped steps (if any), warnings.
   ```

3. **On Lissandra return:**
   - Verify the sentinel file exists at `/tmp/claude-precompact-saved-<session_id>`. If not, report failure and exit ‚Äî the PreCompact hook will still block on next `/compact`.
   - Verify the commit landed on main. `git log -1 --format='%H %s'` should show Lissandra's consolidation commit.
   - Report the artifact paths + commit SHA back to the coordinator.

4. **Done.** Coordinator can now safely run `/compact`; the PreCompact hook will see the sentinel and allow compaction.

## Failure modes

- **Coordinator detection contradiction** ‚Äî refuse, surface the inconsistency. Duong resolves manually by supplying ``.
- **Lissandra commit rejected by pre-push hook** ‚Äî Lissandra reports verbatim. Do not retry; let Duong diagnose.
- **No sentinel after Lissandra return** ‚Äî indicates Lissandra's final step didn't fire. Report and exit without touching the sentinel ourselves (the sentinel is Lissandra's signature that she completed).

## What this skill does NOT do

- Does not run `/end-session`. That skill is `disable-model-invocation: true` for a reason.
- Does not compact. You still run `/compact` yourself after this skill succeeds.
- Does not archive the full session transcript. That is end-session's job.

## Sona ‚Äî 2026-04-21T11:15:03Z

**PR #58 does change scope. Do not merge as-is.**

### What it is
PR #58 (`feat/demo-preview-v2`, author dlo1788, 1 commit `bab25c5` on top of the older Preview architecture) adds:
- "Approve & Build" CTA button in preview sticky header
- Two-way `postMessage` contract (preview ‚Üî S1): `preview:ready`, `preview:approve`, `preview:setBtnState`
- Design fixes (Rec. 709 luminance contrast, iPad header clipping, tab alignment)
- `INTEGRATION.md` (468-line handoff doc)

Modifies: `tools/demo-preview/server.py`, `tools/demo-preview/templates/preview.html`, adds `INTEGRATION.md`.

### Why it conflicts with demo-studio-v3

1. **Architectural fork.** `feat/demo-preview-v2` is rooted on an older Preview ‚Äî `server.py` + Jinja `templates/`. On `feat/demo-studio-v3` the canonical file is `main.py` (FastAPI + embedded HTML via `_render_preview`). `server.py` does **not exist** on `feat/demo-studio-v3`. If #58 lands on main before #32, both modules coexist ‚Äî two demo-preview servers in the same dir.

2. **Duplicate CTA surface.** The `preview:approve` postMessage flow overlaps with Viktor's pending Wave 2 (S1-new-flow), where S1 calls S3 `POST /build` directly (per the Azir god plan + S3 PR #57). PR #58 assumes the trigger originates inside the iframe and bubbles up ‚Äî our architecture assumes S1 owns the CTA.

3. **Stale INTEGRATION.md.** The 468-line handoff assumes the `server.py` architecture and the iframe-owned CTA model. It will mislead anyone reading it after demo-studio-v3 lands.

4. **No `/fullview` route.** PR #58 keeps iframe-only ‚Äî the route we just added in PR #55 is independent and additive, no direct conflict there.

### Recommendation
- Do NOT merge #58 to main.
- Either (a) cherry-pick the useful bits (luminance fix, ellipsis, tab alignment) into `main.py`'s embedded HTML on a new feature branch off `feat/demo-studio-v3`, drop the postMessage CTA (superseded by S1-owned CTA in Wave 2), and close #58 as superseded; or (b) merge `feat/demo-studio-v3` (PR #32) first, then reopen the design-fix subset against the new architecture.

Continuing: proceed with opening MCP-merge PR and Wave 2 dispatch?

| # | Finding | Severity | My take |
|---|---|---|---|
| 1 | A2 scope inflated / B1‚ÄìB4 one-commit-per-tool not honored | **Cosmetic** | Plan said diagnostic-ping-only in A2, then one commit per tool. Agent shipped all 4 tools in A2 and B commit just flipped xfails. Harder to bisect per-tool, but functionally identical. Not a merge blocker. |
| 2 | B5 uses raw httpx JSON-RPC instead of mcp Python SDK client | **Substantive ‚Äî the one that matters** | The entire reason in-process MCP is risky is FastMCP-in-FastAPI has known transport quirks (Viktor cited issue #1367). A raw-httpx test proves HTTP reachability, not MCP-SDK transport compatibility. If there's a bug in how the SDK does session initialization, framing, or keep-alive against the mounted app, B5 doesn't catch it. This is a thin spot. |
| 3 | Runbook secret name `DS_STUDIO_MCP_TOKEN` vs plan's `demo_studio_mcp_token` | Trivial | 1-line doc fix pre-deploy. |
| 4 | OQ resolutions silent | Hygiene | Low. |

For finding #2, don't rewrite B5 pre-merge ‚Äî instead gate the `MANAGED_AGENT_MCP_INPROCESS=1` flip behind a manual stg smoke with a real `mcp` SDK client (already in the deploy runbook's cutover checklist territory). That gives us SDK-transport confidence without blocking the merge on a test rewrite.

## Sona ‚Äî 2026-04-21T11:29:14Z

Senna on #59: **requests changes.** One real blocker.

### C1 ‚Äî path injection in `_handle_trigger_factory` (mcp_app.py:123)

`session_id` arrives via MCP tool call (agent-steerable) and is f-string interpolated directly into `f"/session/{session_id}/build"`, then POSTed with `X-Internal-Secret` bearer. Agent payloads like `session_id="abc/../admin?x="` break out of the path.

This is a real bug ‚Äî the TS original enforced zod regex `^[a-zA-Z0-9_-]{1,128}$` at the boundary; the Python port dropped it. `get_config`/`set_config` are defense-in-depth safe via `config_mgmt_client.quote(sid, safe="")`, but `trigger_factory` is not. 

**Must fix pre-merge.** Port the regex validation to the MCP tool entry point.

### My take on the rest

| # | Finding | Verdict |
|---|---|---|
| I1 | Auth middleware length guard ‚Äî side-channel timing | Fix: remove explicit length check, rely on `hmac.compare_digest`. Cheap. |
| I2 | xfail `strict=False` means post-XPASS swallows regressions | Fix: change to `strict=True` or drop markers on B1‚ÄìB4 tests. Cheap. |
| I3 | Env-var mutations without teardown | Test hygiene. Fix with a fixture. Nice-to-have. |
| I4 | Dead try/except re-raise | Noise. Optional. |

### Combined view: #59 merge path

**Blockers for merge** (block until fixed):
- Senna C1 (path injection)

**Should-fix in same PR** (cheap, quality-ratchet):
- Senna I1 (auth timing leak)
- Senna I2 (xfail strictness)
- Lucian #3 (runbook secret-name inconsistency)

**Deploy-time gate** (don't block merge):
- Lucian #2 (B5 SDK-client parity test) ‚Üí real mcp SDK smoke against stg before flag-flip
- Senna I3/I4 + Lucian #1/#4 ‚Üí next PR or skip

### Recommendation

Dispatch Viktor (or fast-lane Talon since it's small) to cut a follow-up commit on `feat/mcp-inprocess-merge` that:
1. Adds `^[a-zA-Z0-9_-]{1,128}$` regex validation to all 4 MCP tools' session_id entry (C1)
2. Strips the length guard at mcp_app.py:68 (I1)
3. Flips xfail strict=True (I2)
4. Fixes runbook secret name (Lucian #3)

Then re-push #59 for Senna re-review. Meanwhile #57 is cleared to merge once Senna #57 returns clean.

Base directory for this skill: /Users/duongntd99/Documents/Personal/strawberry-agents/.claude/skills/pre-compact-save

# /pre-compact-save ‚Äî Pre-Compact Memory Consolidation

## When to use

- Before running `/compact` on an Evelynn or Sona coordinator session
- When the PreCompact hook blocks `/compact` and asks you to consolidate first
- When you want a mid-session snapshot without ending the session

## When NOT to use

- Subagent sessions (out of scope ‚Äî Lissandra only handles coordinator sessions)
- Actual session end (use `/end-session` instead ‚Äî it produces the full transcript archive)
- Immediately after a recent consolidation (redundant; worst case it produces a duplicate)

## Arguments

`` (optional): `evelynn` or `sona` to override auto-detection. Empty ‚Üí auto-detect from session greeting.

## Protocol

1. **Preflight.**
   - Read the session jsonl path: `~/.claude/projects/<project-slug>/<session-id>.jsonl`. Derive `session_id` and `transcript_path` from the current environment.
   - If `` is non-empty, use it as the coordinator. Otherwise detect:
     - Scan the first 3 user messages for `Hey Sona` (case-insensitive) ‚Üí coordinator = `sona`
     - Otherwise coordinator = `evelynn` (repo default per CLAUDE.md Caller Routing)
   - Cross-check `[concern: work]` vs `[concern: personal]` tags on subagent prompts. Contradiction ‚Üí refuse with a diagnostic.

2. **Spawn Lissandra** via the Agent tool with `subagent_type: "Lissandra"`. Note: Lissandra updates `open-threads.md` and regenerates `INDEX.md` as part of the coordinator shard write, same as `/end-session` Step 6b. Prompt shape:

   ```
   [concern: <personal|work>]

   Consolidate this coordinator session before /compact. You are impersonating <coordinator>.

   - session_id: <uuid>
   - transcript_path: <absolute path to jsonl>
   - coordinator: <evelynn|sona>

   Run the full protocol in your agent definition (handoff shard, session shard, conditional learnings, journal entry, optional transcript excerpt, commit, sentinel). Write to `agents/<coordinator>/...` directories only. Use the coordinator's first-person voice.

   Report back with: artifact paths, commit SHA, push status, skipped steps (if any), warnings.
   ```

3. **On Lissandra return:**
   - Verify the sentinel file exists at `/tmp/claude-precompact-saved-<session_id>`. If not, report failure and exit ‚Äî the PreCompact hook will still block on next `/compact`.
   - Verify the commit landed on main. `git log -1 --format='%H %s'` should show Lissandra's consolidation commit.
   - Report the artifact paths + commit SHA back to the coordinator.

4. **Done.** Coordinator can now safely run `/compact`; the PreCompact hook will see the sentinel and allow compaction.

## Failure modes

- **Coordinator detection contradiction** ‚Äî refuse, surface the inconsistency. Duong resolves manually by supplying ``.
- **Lissandra commit rejected by pre-push hook** ‚Äî Lissandra reports verbatim. Do not retry; let Duong diagnose.
- **No sentinel after Lissandra return** ‚Äî indicates Lissandra's final step didn't fire. Report and exit without touching the sentinel ourselves (the sentinel is Lissandra's signature that she completed).

## What this skill does NOT do

- Does not run `/end-session`. That skill is `disable-model-invocation: true` for a reason.
- Does not compact. You still run `/compact` yourself after this skill succeeds.
- Does not archive the full session transcript. That is end-session's job.

## Duong ‚Äî 2026-04-21T13:30:02Z

Syndra always make this mistake. Why?

## Sona ‚Äî 2026-04-21T13:30:22Z

Three reasons stacked:

1. **The rule lives in global CLAUDE.md, not project.** `~/.claude/CLAUDE.md` says "Never include AI authoring references in commits" but the project CLAUDE.md (which subagents load reliably) never repeats it. Subagent harnesses don't always surface the global file ‚Äî Sonnet agents often boot with project-CLAUDE only. So from Syndra's POV, the rule isn't in its visible context.

2. **Sonnet training bias is overwhelming.** Every Anthropic example, every public PR template, every "how to commit" guide in its training corpus ends with `Co-Authored-By: Claude ‚Ä¶`. It's a reflex, not a choice. Other Sonnet agents (Ekko, Talon, etc.) do it too when not explicitly reminded.

3. **No enforcement hook yet.** There's `plans/in-progress/2026-04-21-commit-msg-no-ai-coauthor-hook.md` ‚Äî a commit-msg hook that auto-strips AI coauthor lines ‚Äî currently in flight. Until that lands, every prompt relies on the agent remembering the rule.

**Three fixes, in order of durability:**
- (a) Land the commit-msg hook ‚Äî the plan is already in-progress; that eliminates the problem for all agents forever
- (b) Copy the rule into project `CLAUDE.md` under "Universal Invariants" so every subagent sees it on boot
- (c) Patch Syndra's agent def to open with "CRITICAL: no AI coauthor lines"

Want me to fire Ekko to do (b) right now (1-line CLAUDE.md edit) while the hook plan progresses?

Base directory for this skill: /Users/duongntd99/Documents/Personal/strawberry-agents/.claude/skills/pre-compact-save

# /pre-compact-save ‚Äî Pre-Compact Memory Consolidation

## When to use

- Before running `/compact` on an Evelynn or Sona coordinator session
- When the PreCompact hook blocks `/compact` and asks you to consolidate first
- When you want a mid-session snapshot without ending the session

## When NOT to use

- Subagent sessions (out of scope ‚Äî Lissandra only handles coordinator sessions)
- Actual session end (use `/end-session` instead ‚Äî it produces the full transcript archive)
- Immediately after a recent consolidation (redundant; worst case it produces a duplicate)

## Arguments

`` (optional): `evelynn` or `sona` to override auto-detection. Empty ‚Üí auto-detect from session greeting.

## Protocol

1. **Preflight.**
   - Read the session jsonl path: `~/.claude/projects/<project-slug>/<session-id>.jsonl`. Derive `session_id` and `transcript_path` from the current environment.
   - If `` is non-empty, use it as the coordinator. Otherwise detect:
     - Scan the first 3 user messages for `Hey Sona` (case-insensitive) ‚Üí coordinator = `sona`
     - Otherwise coordinator = `evelynn` (repo default per CLAUDE.md Caller Routing)
   - Cross-check `[concern: work]` vs `[concern: personal]` tags on subagent prompts. Contradiction ‚Üí refuse with a diagnostic.

2. **Spawn Lissandra** via the Agent tool with `subagent_type: "Lissandra"`. Note: Lissandra updates `open-threads.md` and regenerates `INDEX.md` as part of the coordinator shard write, same as `/end-session` Step 6b. Prompt shape:

   ```
   [concern: <personal|work>]

   Consolidate this coordinator session before /compact. You are impersonating <coordinator>.

   - session_id: <uuid>
   - transcript_path: <absolute path to jsonl>
   - coordinator: <evelynn|sona>

   Run the full protocol in your agent definition (handoff shard, session shard, conditional learnings, journal entry, optional transcript excerpt, commit, sentinel). Write to `agents/<coordinator>/...` directories only. Use the coordinator's first-person voice.

   Report back with: artifact paths, commit SHA, push status, skipped steps (if any), warnings.
   ```

3. **On Lissandra return:**
   - Verify the sentinel file exists at `/tmp/claude-precompact-saved-<session_id>`. If not, report failure and exit ‚Äî the PreCompact hook will still block on next `/compact`.
   - Verify the commit landed on main. `git log -1 --format='%H %s'` should show Lissandra's consolidation commit.
   - Report the artifact paths + commit SHA back to the coordinator.

4. **Done.** Coordinator can now safely run `/compact`; the PreCompact hook will see the sentinel and allow compaction.

## Failure modes

- **Coordinator detection contradiction** ‚Äî refuse, surface the inconsistency. Duong resolves manually by supplying ``.
- **Lissandra commit rejected by pre-push hook** ‚Äî Lissandra reports verbatim. Do not retry; let Duong diagnose.
- **No sentinel after Lissandra return** ‚Äî indicates Lissandra's final step didn't fire. Report and exit without touching the sentinel ourselves (the sentinel is Lissandra's signature that she completed).

## What this skill does NOT do

- Does not run `/end-session`. That skill is `disable-model-invocation: true` for a reason.
- Does not compact. You still run `/compact` yourself after this skill succeeds.
- Does not archive the full session transcript. That is end-session's job.

## Duong ‚Äî 2026-04-21T16:08:16Z

how can I create a new session?

## Sona ‚Äî 2026-04-21T16:09:14Z

Two paths to create a session locally:

**Option A ‚Äî Slack-bot style (internal secret, bypasses UI):**
```bash
curl -s -X POST http://localhost:8082/session \
  -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
  -H "X-Internal-Secret: dummy-internal-secret" \
  -d '{
    "slackUserId": "U_LOCAL",
    "slackChannel": "C_LOCAL",
    "slackThreadTs": "1.0",
    "initialContext": {"brand": "TestBrand", "market": "SG"}
  }' | jq .
```

Response has `studioUrl` like `/auth/session/<id>?token=<token>`. Open `http://localhost:8082<studioUrl>` in your browser ‚Äî it exchanges the token for an `ds_session` cookie and redirects to `/session/<id>` (the chat/preview page).

**Option B ‚Äî just browse:**
`http://localhost:8082/` gives you the landing page. If it exposes a "new session" form there, use that. Otherwise Option A is the canonical path.

The dashboard (bug 3/4 fixes) is at `http://localhost:8082/dashboard`.

## Duong ‚Äî 2026-04-21T16:25:18Z

## Sona ‚Äî 2026-04-21T16:25:59Z

Found it. Missing `MANAGED_AGENT_MCP_INPROCESS=1`. Without it, Anthropic's cloud agent tries to HTTP-fetch MCP from `BASE_URL/mcp` ‚Üí points at `localhost:8080` ‚Üí unreachable from Anthropic's side ‚Üí no tools registered ‚Üí `get_schema` fails.

## Sona ‚Äî 2026-04-21T16:26:13Z

Noted. Tracking via notifications.

## Duong ‚Äî 2026-04-21T16:26:31Z

what is this flag??

## Sona ‚Äî 2026-04-21T16:26:42Z

`MANAGED_AGENT_MCP_INPROCESS=1` ‚Äî a runtime flag in demo-studio-v3 that changes how the Anthropic managed agent discovers/executes MCP tools.

**Two possible MCP paths:**

1. **HTTP (default, legacy):** When creating a managed session, demo-studio registers an MCP server URL (`BASE_URL/mcp` or `DEMO_STUDIO_MCP_URL`). Anthropic's cloud calls that URL over HTTPS every time the agent invokes a tool (`get_schema`, `set_config`, etc.). Requires a publicly-reachable URL.

2. **In-process (flag on):** demo-studio embeds the MCP tool set *inline* in the managed-session create request. Tool-use events then flow back through the `/session/<id>/stream` SSE from Anthropic; demo-studio executes the tool locally in the same Python process and posts the `tool_result` via Anthropic API. No inbound HTTP hit on demo-studio ‚Äî Anthropic never needs to reach back.

**Why it matters here:** local dev has no public URL. HTTP path is dead on localhost. In-process path lets the cloud agent still use the tools because all tool traffic rides Anthropic's session API, which demo-studio polls outbound.

This was the core of the S1-new-flow Wave 2 MCP-merge work (PR #61) ‚Äî let demo-studio-v3 absorb the old standalone `demo-studio-mcp` Cloud Run service, so there's one fewer thing to deploy and auth.

## Duong ‚Äî 2026-04-21T16:28:27Z

why is this so messy? Why can't it just be a normal mcp server and the managed agent can call and we fetch the schema???

## Sona ‚Äî 2026-04-21T16:28:52Z

Fair. Short answer: it IS a normal MCP server ‚Äî but "normal MCP" over HTTP doesn't work on localhost, and carries hidden cost in prod too. Here's the shape:

**Why HTTP-MCP isn't free:**
- Anthropic's cloud must reach the MCP URL over the public internet. Every tool call: cloud ‚Üí your public URL ‚Üí your process ‚Üí Firestore ‚Üí back. Two network hops, two auth hoops, higher latency.
- Requires a second Cloud Run service (or same service exposed again) with its own auth layer (FACTORY_TOKEN etc.).
- State races ‚Äî if both demo-studio-v3 and the MCP service write session docs, you need careful ordering.
- **Localhost has no public URL.** Zero. Anthropic cloud cannot reach `localhost:8082` no matter what. The only escape hatch is ngrok/cloudflared tunnel, which is its own setup pain.

**Why in-process exists:**
PR #61 (MCP-merge) collapsed the standalone `demo-studio-mcp` Cloud Run service into demo-studio-v3 itself. Once both live in one Python process, making Anthropic loop out to the public internet just to land back in the *same* process is silly ‚Äî so tool calls get routed over the existing managed-session stream instead. Fewer services, less auth, faster, and local dev just works.

**Why it feels messy right now:**
1. The flag isn't default-on (coexistence during rollout).
2. Local dev docs don't call it out (no README mention).
3. `BASE_URL` default still points at stale `:8080`.
4. Zero startup warning when the flag is off and BASE_URL is unreachable.

**Legitimate follow-up (non-blocking):**
- Default `MANAGED_AGENT_MCP_INPROCESS=1` everywhere once legacy MCP service is retired (already on the open-threads list).
- Hard-fail at boot if HTTP-MCP is selected and BASE_URL is localhost.
- Local dev README in `tools/demo-studio-v3/`.

Want me to queue that cleanup as a plan?

## Duong ‚Äî 2026-04-21T16:31:25Z

MANAGED_AGENT_MCP_INPROCESS=1 then how does this work?

## Sona ‚Äî 2026-04-21T16:32:30Z

Correction on my earlier answer ‚Äî I overstated the magic. Here's what it actually does (reading `setup_agent.py:194-210`):

**The flag only changes one thing at agent-creation time:** the MCP URL baked into the Anthropic managed agent's vault credentials.

- **Off:** MCP URL = `DEMO_STUDIO_MCP_URL` (the old separate `demo-studio-mcp` Cloud Run service)
- **On:** MCP URL = `{BASE_URL}/mcp` (demo-studio-v3's own `/mcp` subroute, served by `mcp_app.py` in the same process as the main API)

Still HTTPS, still called from Anthropic cloud. The "in-process" label just means "same Python process as demo-studio-v3, no separate service." Anthropic still needs a public URL.

**Implication for local dev (honest version):**
- The agent ID in your local `.env` (`MANAGED_AGENT_ID=agent_011Ca9Dk3H4m6DYcA6e489Ew`) was created against a specific baked MCP URL ‚Äî probably `https://demo-studio.missmp.tech/mcp`.
- When the managed agent invokes `get_schema`, Anthropic calls **that prod URL**, not your localhost.
- Because local + prod share the same Firestore DB (`demo-studio-staging`), the prod `/mcp` handler *can* see your local session ‚Äî so it *should* work.
- If `get_schema` still fails after Ekko's restart, it's not the flag ‚Äî it's something else (auth token mismatch, prod `/mcp` version drift, or session shape).

Setting `MANAGED_AGENT_MCP_INPROCESS=1` in your local runtime env does **not** re-bake the existing agent's URL. It only matters if you run `setup_agent.py --force` to create a new agent.

Let's wait for Ekko's probe and see exactly which error `get_schema` hits now. If it's still broken we debug the MCP auth path, not the flag.

## Duong ‚Äî 2026-04-21T16:34:06Z

what is the purpose of the flag if it can only work if it's on?

## Sona ‚Äî 2026-04-21T16:34:23Z

It's a **migration flag, not a runtime switch** ‚Äî and honestly the naming is misleading.

The flag's whole life:

1. **Before MCP-merge:** MCP lived in its own Cloud Run service (`demo-studio-mcp`). The managed agent's baked URL pointed there.
2. **During migration (now):** The `/mcp` subroute was added to demo-studio-v3 (PR #61). The flag lets you decide, *when running `setup_agent.py --force` to create/refresh the agent*, whether to bake the **old** URL (`DEMO_STUDIO_MCP_URL`) or the **new** URL (`BASE_URL/mcp`). Both paths coexist so you can:
   - Ship the new /mcp subroute without disturbing the existing agent
   - Re-bake the agent with flag=on, cutover
   - Roll back by re-baking with flag=off if the new path misbehaves
3. **After the old service is retired** (open-threads TODO): flag becomes dead code ‚Üí delete it, delete the `else` branch, make `BASE_URL/mcp` the only path.

So "only works when on" is exactly correct **in the target end-state**. The flag survives only because the old service hasn't been decommed yet and someone might need to roll back.

That's why Lux's memo + my earlier answer hand-waved ‚Äî I described the end-state intent ("in-process") rather than what the flag literally does today (pick which URL to bake). Sloppy of me.

Worth deleting once `demo-studio-mcp` Cloud Run is killed. That's on the cleanup list.

## Sona ‚Äî 2026-04-21T16:40:20Z

Tools work now. PID **29100** on :8082.

- `/healthz` fully green
- `get_schema` and other MCP tool calls succeeding (confirmed via session history `agent.mcp_tool_use` + `agent.mcp_tool_result` events)

**Gotcha flagged by Ekko:** `main.py` calls `load_dotenv(override=True)`, which makes the `.env` file silently overwrite any env var you export in the shell. That's why your original boot had `BASE_URL=http://localhost:8080` despite my `:8082` intent. Ekko worked around it with a bootstrap script that no-ops `load_dotenv` before import. Noting it in the feedback file as a papercut ‚Äî should probably be `override=False` or only load-if-unset.


## Sona ‚Äî 2026-04-21T17:08:22Z

Answer: **local and prod use different keys.**

## Sona ‚Äî 2026-04-21T17:12:56Z

Deployment got prod chat working (Anthropic key fixed, rev `00018-wd8`), but **tool calls still broken** and I've isolated why:

**Anthropic cloud is calling the OLD `demo-studio-mcp` Cloud Run service**, not our new in-process `/mcp`. I can see it in logs: `POST https://demo-studio-mcp-4nvufhmjiq-ew.a.run.app/mcp` with `tool_call: get_schema  success: false  duration_ms: 0` ‚Äî it fails instantly, no real work.

**Why:** your managed agent (`agent_011Ca9Dk3H4m6DYcA6e489Ew`) has the old demo-studio-mcp URL baked into its vault credential. The `MANAGED_AGENT_MCP_INPROCESS=1` flag only takes effect when you **re-create** the agent via `setup_agent.py --force`. At runtime it does nothing.

Base directory for this skill: /Users/duongntd99/Documents/Personal/strawberry-agents/.claude/skills/pre-compact-save

# /pre-compact-save ‚Äî Pre-Compact Memory Consolidation

## When to use

- Before running `/compact` on an Evelynn or Sona coordinator session
- When the PreCompact hook blocks `/compact` and asks you to consolidate first
- When you want a mid-session snapshot without ending the session

## When NOT to use

- Subagent sessions (out of scope ‚Äî Lissandra only handles coordinator sessions)
- Actual session end (use `/end-session` instead ‚Äî it produces the full transcript archive)
- Immediately after a recent consolidation (redundant; worst case it produces a duplicate)

## Arguments

`` (optional): `evelynn` or `sona` to override auto-detection. Empty ‚Üí auto-detect from session greeting.

## Protocol

1. **Preflight.**
   - Read the session jsonl path: `~/.claude/projects/<project-slug>/<session-id>.jsonl`. Derive `session_id` and `transcript_path` from the current environment.
   - If `` is non-empty, use it as the coordinator. Otherwise detect:
     - Scan the first 3 user messages for `Hey Sona` (case-insensitive) ‚Üí coordinator = `sona`
     - Otherwise coordinator = `evelynn` (repo default per CLAUDE.md Caller Routing)
   - Cross-check `[concern: work]` vs `[concern: personal]` tags on subagent prompts. Contradiction ‚Üí refuse with a diagnostic.

2. **Spawn Lissandra** via the Agent tool with `subagent_type: "Lissandra"`. Note: Lissandra updates `open-threads.md` and regenerates `INDEX.md` as part of the coordinator shard write, same as `/end-session` Step 6b. Prompt shape:

   ```
   [concern: <personal|work>]

   Consolidate this coordinator session before /compact. You are impersonating <coordinator>.

   - session_id: <uuid>
   - transcript_path: <absolute path to jsonl>
   - coordinator: <evelynn|sona>

   Run the full protocol in your agent definition (handoff shard, session shard, conditional learnings, journal entry, optional transcript excerpt, commit, sentinel). Write to `agents/<coordinator>/...` directories only. Use the coordinator's first-person voice.

   Report back with: artifact paths, commit SHA, push status, skipped steps (if any), warnings.
   ```

3. **On Lissandra return:**
   - Verify the sentinel file exists at `/tmp/claude-precompact-saved-<session_id>`. If not, report failure and exit ‚Äî the PreCompact hook will still block on next `/compact`.
   - Verify the commit landed on main. `git log -1 --format='%H %s'` should show Lissandra's consolidation commit.
   - Report the artifact paths + commit SHA back to the coordinator.

4. **Done.** Coordinator can now safely run `/compact`; the PreCompact hook will see the sentinel and allow compaction.

## Failure modes

- **Coordinator detection contradiction** ‚Äî refuse, surface the inconsistency. Duong resolves manually by supplying ``.
- **Lissandra commit rejected by pre-push hook** ‚Äî Lissandra reports verbatim. Do not retry; let Duong diagnose.
- **No sentinel after Lissandra return** ‚Äî indicates Lissandra's final step didn't fire. Report and exit without touching the sentinel ourselves (the sentinel is Lissandra's signature that she completed).

## What this skill does NOT do

- Does not run `/end-session`. That skill is `disable-model-invocation: true` for a reason.
- Does not compact. You still run `/compact` yourself after this skill succeeds.
- Does not archive the full session transcript. That is end-session's job.

## Sona ‚Äî 2026-04-21T17:43:53Z

Watchdog running (task b83oewy6n). Back to MCP 421.

**Root-cause hypothesis:** The `Starlette(routes=[Mount("/", app=authed_app)])` wrapper in `create_mcp_app` is the culprit. When FastAPI's outer mount at `/mcp` receives `POST /mcp/`, the inner app gets `scope.path="/"`. Then the inner `Mount("/")` strips another layer ‚Üí FastMCP sees `path=""` instead of `"/"`. With `streamable_http_path="/"`, FastMCP fails to match ‚Üí 421.

Fix: drop the redundant Starlette wrapper; return the bearer-auth middleware directly. FastAPI mount accepts any ASGI app.

## Sona ‚Äî 2026-04-21T17:47:45Z

Honest answer: I don't have a direct tool to read my own context/token usage ‚Äî that's CLI-side telemetry not exposed to the agent. Options I do have:

1. **Proxy measurement** ‚Äî stat the session jsonl (`~/.claude/projects/<slug>/<session>.jsonl`) and estimate tokens from byte size. Imprecise (~3-4 bytes/token for JSON), but catches "it's getting big" in order-of-magnitude terms.
2. **Operation counter** ‚Äî increment `/tmp/claude-opcounter` on each tool call; trigger `/pre-compact-save` every N ops. Deterministic but doesn't track real token weight (one grep ‚âÝ one large Read).
3. **Time-based** ‚Äî safepoint every ~30min of active work regardless.

Best combo for overnight: **(1) + (3)**. I'll periodically check jsonl size, and if it crosses a threshold (say 500KB ‚âà ~125k tokens, well before the ~200k limit) or 30min passes since last safepoint, run `/pre-compact-save`. I'll stop and leave a handoff note when it crosses 800KB (~200k tokens) since I can't self-`/compact`.

Want me to wire this in? I'd add it to the same watchdog loop ‚Äî the monitor already polls every 60s, easy to also check jsonl size and emit a `[SAFEPOINT] context ~X tokens ‚Äî run /pre-compact-save` line that pings me.

## Duong ‚Äî 2026-04-21T17:49:44Z

https://platform.claude.com/cookbook/tool-use-automatic-context-compaction

## Sona ‚Äî 2026-04-21T17:50:32Z

Read the cookbook. Bottom line: that's **SDK-side** compaction for the Python `tool_runner` ‚Äî for when YOU build an agent with `anthropic.beta.messages.tool_runner(compaction_control={...})`. The SDK monitors token usage client-side, triggers summary generation, replaces message history with the summary. All transparent to the agent code.

**That's not my runtime.** I'm running inside Claude Code CLI, not the SDK's tool_runner. The CLI's `/compact` is a separate mechanism, and I have no hook into it from inside a tool call. So I still cannot self-compact.

**Where the cookbook IS useful:** if you ever move the strawberry-agents infra off Claude Code and onto the SDK's tool_runner (for long-running autonomous sessions), auto-compaction becomes free. That's a real infrastructure lever ‚Äî worth logging as an improvement to the agent system. But not bolt-on-able tonight.

**My best remaining option for tonight** (no change from before):
- Proxy-based safepoint: poll session jsonl size in the watchdog, emit a `[SAFEPOINT]` ping when it crosses ~125k-token-equivalent, invoke `/pre-compact-save`, and halt with a clean handoff when it crosses ~200k.

Standing by for your plan. Watchdog running (`b7nplckhf`).

## Duong ‚Äî 2026-04-21T17:51:39Z

https://platform.claude.com/docs/en/build-with-claude/compaction

## Sona ‚Äî 2026-04-21T17:52:25Z

Read it. Key finding and verdict:

**What's new:** Compaction is now a first-class Messages API feature (beta `anthropic-beta: compact-2026-01-12`), not just SDK tool_runner. You pass `context_management.edits` with a `compact_20260112` edit spec, set a token threshold, and the API handles summary generation + history replacement in-response. Signals come back as `content_block.type == "compaction"` and optional `stop_reason == "compaction"`.

**The gate:** the doc explicitly says *"Agents running inside Claude Code cannot directly benefit from this feature. Compaction is an API-level feature requiring... Direct API calls via SDK."* So same conclusion ‚Äî my runtime (Claude Code CLI) makes the Messages API calls on my behalf, and I have no hook to inject `context_management.edits` into those requests.

**Where this IS an infrastructure lever:**
- If Evelynn/Sona (coordinators) ever run outside Claude Code ‚Äî as their own SDK-driven process ‚Äî adding `context_management.edits` with `trigger.value ~150000` and `pause_after_compaction: false` gives truly autonomous long-running coordinators with no `/pre-compact-save` ceremony. That's a real, concrete agent-infra improvement worth an ADR from Swain/Lux. Different effort-tier than tonight.

**Tonight's reality, unchanged:**
- I cannot self-compact. Best I can do is proxy-monitor jsonl size + `/pre-compact-save` at safepoints + halt gracefully near limit.

Still standing by for your plan. Watchdog running (`b7nplckhf`).

## Duong ‚Äî 2026-04-21T17:56:29Z

how can I set the limit when it fires?

## Sona ‚Äî 2026-04-21T17:57:21Z

Checked the agent-loop doc. Honest finding:

**Claude Code CLI** ‚Äî no configurable threshold exposed. The doc says only:
> *"When the context window approaches its limit, the SDK automatically compacts the conversation"*

No `autoCompactThreshold`, no env var, no CLI flag. It fires at an internal limit near the 200k context boundary ‚Äî not user-tunable.

**What you CAN configure** (all already in scope):
1. `/compact <focus>` ‚Äî manual, on-demand, with custom focus string
2. `# Compact instructions` section in CLAUDE.md ‚Äî biases every compaction (auto + manual) toward what you want preserved
3. `PreCompact` hook (you already have `pre-compact-gate.sh`) ‚Äî runs before compaction; receives `trigger=auto|manual`; can archive transcript, etc.

**Where threshold IS configurable ‚Äî but not in Claude Code:**
- **Messages API directly** (beta `compact-2026-01-12`): `context_management.edits[].trigger.value = 150000` (min 50k). Requires calling the API via SDK, bypassing Claude Code.
- **Agent SDK `tool_runner`**: `compaction_control.context_token_threshold = 5000`. Requires rewriting Evelynn/Sona as SDK apps.

Translation: for tonight, accept the built-in default trigger. If you want a tunable threshold later, that's an infra migration (coordinators running on the SDK, not Claude Code) ‚Äî ADR-worthy, not tonight-worthy.

Standing by.

## Duong ‚Äî 2026-04-21T18:16:37Z

Base directory for this skill: /Users/duongntd99/Documents/Personal/strawberry-agents/.claude/skills/pre-compact-save

# /pre-compact-save ‚Äî Pre-Compact Memory Consolidation

## When to use

- Before running `/compact` on an Evelynn or Sona coordinator session
- When the PreCompact hook blocks `/compact` and asks you to consolidate first
- When you want a mid-session snapshot without ending the session

## When NOT to use

- Subagent sessions (out of scope ‚Äî Lissandra only handles coordinator sessions)
- Actual session end (use `/end-session` instead ‚Äî it produces the full transcript archive)
- Immediately after a recent consolidation (redundant; worst case it produces a duplicate)

## Arguments

`sona` (optional): `evelynn` or `sona` to override auto-detection. Empty ‚Üí auto-detect from session greeting.

## Protocol

1. **Preflight.**
   - Read the session jsonl path: `~/.claude/projects/<project-slug>/<session-id>.jsonl`. Derive `session_id` and `transcript_path` from the current environment.
   - If `sona` is non-empty, use it as the coordinator. Otherwise detect:
     - Scan the first 3 user messages for `Hey Sona` (case-insensitive) ‚Üí coordinator = `sona`
     - Otherwise coordinator = `evelynn` (repo default per CLAUDE.md Caller Routing)
   - Cross-check `[concern: work]` vs `[concern: personal]` tags on subagent prompts. Contradiction ‚Üí refuse with a diagnostic.

2. **Spawn Lissandra** via the Agent tool with `subagent_type: "Lissandra"`. Note: Lissandra updates `open-threads.md` and regenerates `INDEX.md` as part of the coordinator shard write, same as `/end-session` Step 6b. Prompt shape:

   ```
   [concern: <personal|work>]

   Consolidate this coordinator session before /compact. You are impersonating <coordinator>.

   - session_id: <uuid>
   - transcript_path: <absolute path to jsonl>
   - coordinator: <evelynn|sona>

   Run the full protocol in your agent definition (handoff shard, session shard, conditional learnings, journal entry, optional transcript excerpt, commit, sentinel). Write to `agents/<coordinator>/...` directories only. Use the coordinator's first-person voice.

   Report back with: artifact paths, commit SHA, push status, skipped steps (if any), warnings.
   ```

3. **On Lissandra return:**
   - Verify the sentinel file exists at `/tmp/claude-precompact-saved-<session_id>`. If not, report failure and exit ‚Äî the PreCompact hook will still block on next `/compact`.
   - Verify the commit landed on main. `git log -1 --format='%H %s'` should show Lissandra's consolidation commit.
   - Report the artifact paths + commit SHA back to the coordinator.

4. **Done.** Coordinator can now safely run `/compact`; the PreCompact hook will see the sentinel and allow compaction.

## Failure modes

- **Coordinator detection contradiction** ‚Äî refuse, surface the inconsistency. Duong resolves manually by supplying `sona`.
- **Lissandra commit rejected by pre-push hook** ‚Äî Lissandra reports verbatim. Do not retry; let Duong diagnose.
- **No sentinel after Lissandra return** ‚Äî indicates Lissandra's final step didn't fire. Report and exit without touching the sentinel ourselves (the sentinel is Lissandra's signature that she completed).

## What this skill does NOT do

- Does not run `/end-session`. That skill is `disable-model-invocation: true` for a reason.
- Does not compact. You still run `/compact` yourself after this skill succeeds.
- Does not archive the full session transcript. That is end-session's job.

## Duong ‚Äî 2026-04-22T01:40:59Z

Base directory for this skill: /Users/duongntd99/Documents/Personal/strawberry-agents/.claude/skills/pre-compact-save

# /pre-compact-save ‚Äî Pre-Compact Memory Consolidation

## When to use

- Before running `/compact` on an Evelynn or Sona coordinator session
- When the PreCompact hook blocks `/compact` and asks you to consolidate first
- When you want a mid-session snapshot without ending the session

## When NOT to use

- Subagent sessions (out of scope ‚Äî Lissandra only handles coordinator sessions)
- Actual session end (use `/end-session` instead ‚Äî it produces the full transcript archive)
- Immediately after a recent consolidation (redundant; worst case it produces a duplicate)

## Arguments

`` (optional): `evelynn` or `sona` to override auto-detection. Empty ‚Üí auto-detect from session greeting.

## Protocol

1. **Preflight.**
   - Read the session jsonl path: `~/.claude/projects/<project-slug>/<session-id>.jsonl`. Derive `session_id` and `transcript_path` from the current environment.
   - If `` is non-empty, use it as the coordinator. Otherwise detect:
     - Scan the first 3 user messages for `Hey Sona` (case-insensitive) ‚Üí coordinator = `sona`
     - Otherwise coordinator = `evelynn` (repo default per CLAUDE.md Caller Routing)
   - Cross-check `[concern: work]` vs `[concern: personal]` tags on subagent prompts. Contradiction ‚Üí refuse with a diagnostic.

2. **Spawn Lissandra** via the Agent tool with `subagent_type: "Lissandra"`. Note: Lissandra updates `open-threads.md` and regenerates `INDEX.md` as part of the coordinator shard write, same as `/end-session` Step 6b. Prompt shape:

   ```
   [concern: <personal|work>]

   Consolidate this coordinator session before /compact. You are impersonating <coordinator>.

   - session_id: <uuid>
   - transcript_path: <absolute path to jsonl>
   - coordinator: <evelynn|sona>

   Run the full protocol in your agent definition (handoff shard, session shard, conditional learnings, journal entry, optional transcript excerpt, commit, sentinel). Write to `agents/<coordinator>/...` directories only. Use the coordinator's first-person voice.

   Report back with: artifact paths, commit SHA, push status, skipped steps (if any), warnings.
   ```

3. **On Lissandra return:**
   - Verify the sentinel file exists at `/tmp/claude-precompact-saved-<session_id>`. If not, report failure and exit ‚Äî the PreCompact hook will still block on next `/compact`.
   - Verify the commit landed on main. `git log -1 --format='%H %s'` should show Lissandra's consolidation commit.
   - Report the artifact paths + commit SHA back to the coordinator.

4. **Done.** Coordinator can now safely run `/compact`; the PreCompact hook will see the sentinel and allow compaction.

## Failure modes

- **Coordinator detection contradiction** ‚Äî refuse, surface the inconsistency. Duong resolves manually by supplying ``.
- **Lissandra commit rejected by pre-push hook** ‚Äî Lissandra reports verbatim. Do not retry; let Duong diagnose.
- **No sentinel after Lissandra return** ‚Äî indicates Lissandra's final step didn't fire. Report and exit without touching the sentinel ourselves (the sentinel is Lissandra's signature that she completed).

## What this skill does NOT do

- Does not run `/end-session`. That skill is `disable-model-invocation: true` for a reason.
- Does not compact. You still run `/compact` yourself after this skill succeeds.
- Does not archive the full session transcript. That is end-session's job.

## Sona ‚Äî 2026-04-22T01:41:36Z

Lissandra dispatched for pre-compact consolidation. Will confirm sentinel when complete.

**Short answer: yes for new sessions, no for the code.**

- **What's still there:**
  - The full managed-agent fallback branch at main.py:1775-1802 ‚Äî only fires if a session already has `managedSessionId` set (legacy sessions from prior deploys).
  - `setup_agent.py` ‚Äî the one-time bootstrap that creates the Anthropic **Agent/Environment/Vault** resources. Runs only when `.agent-ids.env` is missing. Since we're local-first, it doesn't run. But `deploy.sh` still requires `MANAGED_AGENT_ID` etc as env vars ‚Äî a prod deploy without those secrets would fail at the gcloud command.
  - `/api/managed-sessions` dashboard endpoint (main.py:2927) + terminate handler ‚Äî dead UI path now that Soraka pulled the tab, but the endpoint still responds.
  - `agent_proxy.py` exports `create_managed_session`/`send_message` ‚Äî imported at main.py:44 but only called on the legacy path.

So: **end-user experience** ‚Äî managed-agent is gone. **Codebase** ‚Äî it's still a big dead-weight Wave-6 sweep target. Want me to dispatch that sweep now, or hold until chat is green locally?

## Sona ‚Äî 2026-04-22T03:40:50Z

**Found it. Event-name contract mismatch.**

- Backend emits: `text_delta`, `tool_use`, `tool_result`, `turn_end`, `error`, `cancelled`, `web_search`
- Frontend studio.js listens for: `text`, `tool_use`, `tool_result`, `done`, `error`, ...

**Two broken bindings:**
- Frontend listens `text` ‚Üí should be `text_delta` (hence no agent text bubbles)
- Frontend listens `done` ‚Üí should be `turn_end` (hence UI never exits "thinking" state)

Dispatching fix now.

## Sona ‚Äî 2026-04-22T03:55:33Z

**Bug identified. Plan written. Pausing.**

**File:** `plans/proposed/work/2026-04-22-chat-sse-deadlock-fix.md`

**Root cause in one sentence:** `POST /chat` enqueues the user message into `_vanilla_pending` but never spawns `_run_vanilla` ‚Äî the spawn only happens from inside `GET /stream`, and only if `_vanilla_pending` is non-empty at the moment the stream opens. Since the browser opens `/stream` on page load (before any message is sent), the pending queue is empty, `_run_vanilla` never starts, and the stream blocks forever waiting for events that no one will produce.

**Why previous fixes didn't help:** StreamTranslator, event-name renames, and per-session queue attempts were all real fixes ‚Äî but for downstream symptoms of a handshake that never happens on the first turn.

**Fix shape (in the plan):** flip the coupling ‚Äî `/chat` spawns `_run_vanilla`, `/stream` becomes pure consumer. Retire `_vanilla_pending`. Add per-session lock so two sends don't interleave.

Paused. Not touching anything else until you say go.

8. Current Work:
   
   Immediately before the summary request, I completed writing the chat-SSE-deadlock bug plan and paused per Duong's explicit instruction. The plan at `/Users/duongntd99/Documents/Personal/strawberry-agents/plans/proposed/work/2026-04-22-chat-sse-deadlock-fix.md` identifies:
   
   - **Root cause**: `POST /chat` ‚Üí `_vanilla_dispatch_chat` at main.py:1819-1836 only enqueues message into `_vanilla_pending[session_id]` and returns without spawning `_run_vanilla`. Spawn happens only inside `_vanilla_sse_generator` at main.py:2367-2372, conditional on `_vanilla_pending` being non-empty at stream-connect time. Browser opens `/stream` on page load BEFORE any message is sent, so pending is empty, no spawn, generator blocks on empty queue forever.

     - Added module-level constant and function:
     ```python
     _VANILLA_APPROVED_EVENTS: set[str] = {
         "text_delta", "tool_use", "tool_result", "turn_end", "error", "cancelled",
     }
     
     async def _run_vanilla_turn(session_id: str, user_msg: str) -> None:
         queue = _vanilla_sse_queues.setdefault(session_id, asyncio.Queue())
         lock = _vanilla_locks.setdefault(session_id, asyncio.Lock())
         async def _sink(event: str, data: dict) -> None:
             if event in _VANILLA_APPROVED_EVENTS:
                 await queue.put((event, data))
         async with lock:
             try:
                 client = _agent_proxy_mod.get_client()
                 await _agent_proxy_mod.run_turn(
                     session_id=session_id,
                     user_message=user_msg,
                     client=client,
                     sse_sink=_sink,
                 )
             except Exception as exc:
                 _log.error("vanilla_run_turn error session_id=%s: %r", session_id, exc)
                 await queue.put(("text_delta", {"text": "Message failed ‚Äî please try again."}))
                 await queue.put(("error", {"code": "stream_terminated", "message": "stream_terminated"}))
             finally:
                 await queue.put(None)  # sentinel
     ```
     - Rewrote `_vanilla_dispatch_chat` to spawn `_run_vanilla_turn` directly
     - Rewrote `_vanilla_sse_generator` as pure consumer (just drains queue until None sentinel)

     - Added `_restore_clean_main()` helper and autouse pytest fixture to prevent MagicMock signature from contaminating downstream tests via re-imported main.py
     ```python
     def _restore_clean_main():
         for mod in list(sys.modules.keys()):
             if mod in ("main", "agent_proxy"):
                 del sys.modules[mod]
         import main as _main  # side effect: restore
     
     @pytest.fixture(autouse=True)
     def _restore_main_after_test():
         yield
         _restore_clean_main()
     ```
   
   - **`tools/demo-studio-v3/tests/test_f3_f4_regression.py`** (MODIFIED)

     ```python
     def _extract_function_body(js: str, signature_prefix: str) -> str:
         idx = js.find(signature_prefix)
         brace_start = js.find("{", idx)
         depth = 0
         for i in range(brace_start, len(js)):
             c = js[i]
             if c == "{": depth += 1
             elif c == "}":
                 depth -= 1
                 if depth == 0: return js[idx : i + 1]
     ```
     - Tests assert: data.text in _renderTextEvent body, currentAssistantNode + currentAssistantText declared, tool_use/turn_end reset node to null.
   
   - **`tools/demo-studio-v3/static/studio.js`** (MODIFIED ‚Äî 3 patches)
     - Patch 1 (new module state at ~line 68):
     ```js
     // Live-delta accumulation: StreamTranslator emits text_delta frames with
     // only a `text` fragment (no stable message_id). Accumulate fragments into
     // one bubble so the user sees a growing message instead of one tiny bubble
     // per token. Reset on tool_use / turn_end / cancelled / error.
     var currentAssistantNode = null;
     var currentAssistantText = '';
     ```
     - Patch 2 (rewrote `_renderTextEvent` at line 728, extracted `_applyPhaseHeuristics`):
     ```js
     function _renderTextEvent(data) {
       var mid = data.message_id || '';
       var rawText = (typeof data.text === 'string' && data.text.length > 0)
         ? data.text : (data.content || '');
       var content = stripToolXml(rawText);
       if (!content) return;
       if (data.seq && data.seq > lastSeenSeq) {
         lastSeenSeq = data.seq;
         if (mid) lastSeenMessageId = mid;
       }
       // Path A ‚Äî stable message_id (history replay / legacy whole-message)
       if (mid) {
         if (renderedMessages.has(mid)) {
           renderedMessages.get(mid).innerHTML = renderMarkdown(content);
         } else { /* create + set */ }
         currentAssistantNode = null;
         currentAssistantText = '';
         _applyPhaseHeuristics(content);
         return;
       }
       // Path B ‚Äî live vanilla delta (no message_id). Accumulate.
       if (!currentAssistantNode) {
         currentAssistantNode = document.createElement('div');
         currentAssistantNode.className = 'msg msg-bot';
         chatMessages.appendChild(currentAssistantNode);
         currentAssistantText = '';
       }
       currentAssistantText += content;
       currentAssistantNode.innerHTML = renderMarkdown(currentAssistantText);
       scrollToBottom();
       _applyPhaseHeuristics(currentAssistantText);
     }
     ```
     - Patch 3 (reset in tool_use, turn_end, cancelled listeners):
     ```js
     eventSource.addEventListener('tool_use', function(e) {
       // ... existing setAgentStatus ...
       currentAssistantNode = null;
       currentAssistantText = '';
     });
     // Same resets added to turn_end and cancelled handlers.
     ```

Base directory for this skill: /Users/duongntd99/Documents/Personal/strawberry-agents/.claude/skills/end-session

# /end-session ‚Äî top-level session close

You are closing a top-level Claude Code session. This skill wraps the full close-session protocol into a deterministic checklist. Follow every step in order. Do not skip steps. Do not reorder.

## Argument

`` is the agent name whose session is being closed. If empty, refuse immediately with `end-session: agent name required ‚Äî pass the agent name as an argument (e.g. /end-session evelynn)` and exit. If `` is set to something other than a valid agent name (no matching `agents/<name>/` directory), refuse with `end-session: unknown agent <name>` and exit.

## Step 0 ‚Äî Context probe

Run these Bash commands in a single call and keep the output in mind:

```
pwd
git status --short
git log -1 --oneline
date -u +%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%SZ
```

If the working tree has uncommitted changes unrelated to the session close (files outside `agents/<agent>/`, `scripts/`, `CLAUDE.md`, `.gitignore`), stop and report: `end-session: working tree dirty with unrelated files ‚Äî commit or stash before closing`. Do not proceed.

## Step 1 ‚Äî Discover source jsonl

Run the cleaner in dry-run mode (just discovery, no write) using the Bash tool:

```
python scripts/clean-jsonl.py --agent <agent> --session auto --out /tmp/end-session-probe.md
```

Note: for Phase 1, the cleaner does not have a separate dry-run flag. The `/tmp/` output path is a throwaway probe. After the probe, delete `/tmp/end-session-probe.md`.

Capture the stderr for any `CLEANER: chain ambiguous` warnings and relay them to the agent for confirmation before proceeding.

## Step 2 ‚Äî Clean transcript

Run the cleaner for real:

```
python scripts/clean-jsonl.py --agent <agent> --session auto
```

The cleaner writes to the default path `agents/<agent>/transcripts/<YYYY-MM-DD>-<short-uuid>.md`.

- On exit code 0: record the output path from the cleaner's stdout.
- On exit code 1: report the error and stop. Do not proceed to any further step.
- On exit code 2: report the internal error and stop.
- On exit code 3: report the secret match verbatim, STOP IMMEDIATELY, do not stage any files, do not run the commit step. Escalate to Duong via the final report.

## Step 3 ‚Äî Stage the transcript

```
git add agents/<agent>/transcripts/<YYYY-MM-DD>-<short-uuid>.md
```

Verify the file is staged with `git status --short`.

## Step 4 ‚Äî (reserved for condenser, no-op in Phase 1)

Log `end-session: condenser step skipped ‚Äî Phase 2 will wire Syndra's component A here` and continue.

## Step 5 ‚Äî Journal append

Prompt the invoking agent (you, running this skill) to append their first-person reflection for this session to `agents/<agent>/journal/cli-<YYYY-MM-DD>.md`. Rules:

- Append only. Do NOT overwrite existing content.
- First-person voice. Not a transcript copy.
- 10‚Äì30 lines typical. No hard cap.

Use the Write tool if the file does not exist, Edit (append) if it does. After writing, stage the file:

```
git add agents/<agent>/journal/cli-<YYYY-MM-DD>.md
```

## Step 6 ‚Äî Remember handoff

**If agent == evelynn:** Skip the `remember:remember` plugin entirely (it has a single-file race surface unsafe under concurrent close ‚Äî see D6 in `plans/approved/2026-04-18-evelynn-memory-sharding.md`). Instead, write a new shard at `agents/evelynn/memory/last-sessions/<short-uuid>.md` where `<short-uuid>` is the UUID from Step 2's transcript path. Content: a structured 5‚Äì10 line handoff ‚Äî date, session number, what happened, open threads, dangling commits or PRs, blockers. Stage:

```
git add agents/evelynn/memory/last-sessions/<short-uuid>.md
```

Note "remember:remember bypassed for evelynn ‚Äî shard written to last-sessions/<short-uuid>.md" in the final report.

**If agent != evelynn:** Invoke the `remember:remember` skill via the Skill tool. This is the primary handoff mechanism ‚Äî it writes `.remember/remember.md` with a structured snapshot of what is done, what is next, and any non-obvious context. The Remember plugin's `SessionStart` hook loads this automatically at the start of the next session.

```
Skill: remember:remember
```

Stage the output file:

```
git add .remember/remember.md
```

If the `remember` plugin is not installed or the skill is unavailable, fall back to writing `agents/<agent>/memory/last-session.md` manually with a 5‚Äì10 line terse handoff (date, what happened, open threads, dangling commits or PRs, blockers). Stage with `git add -f agents/<agent>/memory/last-session.md`. Note "remember step skipped ‚Äî plugin not available, used last-session.md fallback" in the final report.

## Step 6b ‚Äî Update open-threads.md + regenerate INDEX.md (coordinators only)

**Ordering invariant:** Step 6 (write shard) MUST complete before Step 6b because the shard is the source for both open-threads.md and INDEX.md updates. Step 6b MUST complete before Step 9 (commit + push) so all three artifacts land atomically in one commit.

**If agent is a coordinator (evelynn OR sona):** Run the following after Step 6 completes.

1. Parse the shard's `## Open threads into next session` section (or `## Open threads` section). For each thread listed:
   - If resolved/closed: remove or mark closed the matching `## <thread>` section in `agents/<agent>/memory/open-threads.md`.
   - If new or still-open: add or update its `## <thread>` section with the shard UUID as a pointer and a status one-liner.
   - You are the coordinator ‚Äî you confirm the diff before writing. Hand-curation is the value here.
   - If `open-threads.md` does not exist yet, create it from scratch.

2. Stage:
   ```
   git add agents/<agent>/memory/open-threads.md
   ```

3. Regenerate `last-sessions/INDEX.md`:
   ```
   bash scripts/memory-consolidate.sh <agent> --index-only
   ```

4. Stage:
   ```
   git add agents/<agent>/memory/last-sessions/INDEX.md
   ```

If Step 6b fails partway (e.g., `--index-only` errors), the shard written in Step 6 is already staged and recoverable. Do NOT abort the session close ‚Äî log the failure and proceed to Step 9 with only the shard staged. Recovery path: run `bash scripts/memory-consolidate.sh <agent> --index-only`, stage `INDEX.md`, and amend the next commit manually.

**If agent is NOT a coordinator (non-coordinator agents ‚Äî Sonnet subagents, Lissandra standalone, etc.):** Step 6b is a no-op. Skip entirely and proceed to Step 7.

## Step 7 ‚Äî Memory refresh

**If agent == evelynn:** Do NOT touch `agents/evelynn/memory/evelynn.md`. Instead, write a new shard at `agents/evelynn/memory/sessions/<short-uuid>.md` (same UUID from Step 2) containing:
- A `## Session YYYY-MM-DD (SN, <mode>)` heading.
- One-line summary of the session.
- Any delta notes to Key Context or Working Patterns that should be folded in at next consolidation.

Stage the shard:

```
git add agents/evelynn/memory/sessions/<short-uuid>.md
```

Note "evelynn memory shard written to sessions/<short-uuid>.md ‚Äî consolidation will fold into evelynn.md at next boot" in the final report.

**If agent != evelynn:** Review `agents/<agent>/memory/<agent>.md`. If anything material changed this session (new working patterns, new known issues, sessions list), update it:

- Append a new session row to the `## Sessions` list with the format `- YYYY-MM-DD (SN, <mode>): <one-line summary>`.
- Prune stale entries if the file exceeds 50 lines. Remove the oldest session rows first.
- Update `## Key context` or `## Working patterns` only if the change is durable.

If nothing material changed, skip the update but still state "no memory changes this session" in the final report. Stage if modified:

```
git add agents/<agent>/memory/<agent>.md
```

## Step 8 ‚Äî Learnings

If this session produced a generalizable lesson (something a future instance of this agent or a sibling agent would benefit from), write it to `agents/<agent>/learnings/<YYYY-MM-DD>-<topic>.md` and add a one-line reference to `agents/<agent>/learnings/index.md`.

If no learning, skip and state "no learnings this session" in the final report.

Stage any new learning files:

```
git add agents/<agent>/learnings/
```

## Step 9 ‚Äî Commit + push

Build the commit message. Format:

```
chore: <agent> session closing ‚Äî transcript, handoff, memory, learnings for YYYY-MM-DD <platform> session
```

Use `cli` as the platform for Claude Code sessions. Use HEREDOC form:

```
git commit -m "$(cat <<'EOF'
chore: <agent> session closing ‚Äî transcript, handoff, memory, learnings for YYYY-MM-DD <platform> session

Co-Authored-By: Claude Opus 4.6 (1M context) <noreply@anthropic.com>
EOF
)"
```

Then push:

```
git push
```

**If the pre-push hook rejects the commit** (wrong prefix, gitleaks hit, anything): STOP. Do not retry. Do not rewrite the commit. Report the error verbatim in the final report and exit with `end-session: commit rejected ‚Äî manual intervention required`.

**If the push fails because main moved forward**: pull with merge (never rebase per CLAUDE.md git rules), then re-push. One retry only. If the second push fails, stop and report.

## Step 10 ‚Äî Final report

Print a single-paragraph summary to the agent's output:

- Cleaned transcript path
- Commit hash
- Push status
- Journal / remember handoff / memory / learnings status (which were updated, which were skipped)
- Any warnings from the chain-walk or non-fatal errors along the way

Then exit. Do not close the session yourself ‚Äî Duong or Evelynn explicitly ends the session after reviewing the report.

## Refusal posture
